def confirmSign(
action: String,
additionalRequestName: String = ""
): ChainBuilder = {
builder
.exec(session => {
val formNode = session("formNode").as[Node]
val selector = new NodeSelector(formNode)
val actions = mutable.Map[String, String]()
selector
.select("button[name='actionBar:applyButton']")
.asScala
.foreach(node => {
actions.put("confirm", node.getAttribute("name"))
})
selector
.select("button[name='actionBar:cancelButton']")
.asScala
.foreach(node => {
actions.put("cancel", node.getAttribute("name"))
})
var newSession =
session
.set("actions", actions.asJava)
.set(
"formPostUrl",
formNode
.getAttribute("action")
.substring(formNode.getAttribute("action").lastIndexOf("."))
)
val defaultActionNodes = selector.select("button.cancel").asScala
if (defaultActionNodes.size == 1) {
newSession = newSession.set(
"Cancel",
defaultActionNodes.head.getAttribute("name")
)
}
newSession
})
.exec(
http("Confirm " + additionalRequestName).nextStep
.withAction(action)
)
.standardPause
.exec(saveActionNameInSession(".done"))
.execPageAction(
".done",
"click",
http("Close signing result")
.doActionPost("1")
.checkAjaxResponse)
.reloadCurrentPage("after confirming")
}

Preinit Pool
The connection pool can be initialized instantly. If set to False (default), the JDBC request samplers using this pool might measure higher response times for the first queries ‚Äì as the connection establishment time for the whole pool is included.
